plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:20:#   - Player head tool: Set's an armor stand's head to the head of a specified player.
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:25:#   /astools                        Give yourself all of the armor stand tools (Note: Clears your inventory)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:26:#   /astools reload                 Reload the armor stand tools plugin config file
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:29:#                                   Add an assigned command to the nearest armor stand. See the assigning commands section below for more info.
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:30:#   /ascmd remove <command_number>  Remove the command assigned to the nearest armor stand
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:31:#   /ascmd list                     List the commands assigned to the nearest armor stand
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:32:#   /ascmd cooldown <ticks>         Set the cooldown for the command on nearest armor stand (Setting this overrides the default cooldown from config.yml)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:33:#   /ascmd cooldown remove          Remove the cooldown for the command on nearest armor stand (Default cooldown set in config.yml will be used)

plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:41:#   astools.summon                  Permission to use the summon tool (Summons an armor stand without requiring the materials)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:42:#   astools.head                    Permission to use the player head tool (Ability to specify a player head for an armor stand)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:44:#   astools.glow                    Permission to use the glow tool (Glow effect on armor stands)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:45:#   astools.ascmd.add.console       Permission to add a console command to an armor stand (Previously astools.ascmd.assign.console)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:46:#   astools.ascmd.add.player        Permission to add a player command to an armor stand (Previously astools.ascmd.assign.player)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:47:#   astools.ascmd.add.bungee        Permission to add a bungee command to an armor stand (See below for details)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:48:#   astools.ascmd.remove            Permission to remove a command from an armor stand
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:49:#   astools.ascmd.list              Permission to list the commands assigned to an armor stand  (Previously astools.ascmd.view)
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:50:#   astools.ascmd.cooldown          Permission to add/remove a cooldown to commands assigned to an armor stand
plugins/ArmorStandTools/config.yml:51:#   astools.ascmd.execute           Permission to execute commands assigned to an armor stand by (on right click)
